[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput archive allow writes outside the intended output directory.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Observed  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m feeds crafted archive [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata into `[0m[1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJazzer’s `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer detects an attempt to write to a path [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutside the target directory [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-tmp[0m[39m…[0m[35m/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and throws [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is a file path traversal vulnerability. Unvalidated or insufficiently [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitized entry names in the archive permit directory traversal [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `..[0m[35m/[0m[39m` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that break out of the intended extraction directory.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations and Findings  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception is raised in [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.check` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m346[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating that a path check failed.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The violation is detected specifically in [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FilePathTraversal.copyMismatchMvHook` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m211[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m after path validation logic in [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness itself [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` at line [0m[1;36m52[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is only an [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
